\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a5002af34dc323ff28e87ae83203b2c36}\index{tf@{tf}!atomic\_max@{atomic\_max}}
\index{atomic\_max@{atomic\_max}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{atomic\_max()}{atomic\_max()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a5002af34dc323ff28e87ae83203b2c36} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::atomic\+\_\+max (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::atomic$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}} $>$ \&}]{v}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}} \&}]{max\+\_\+v}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}



updates an atomic variable with the maximum value 

This function atomically updates the provided atomic variable {\ttfamily v} to hold the maximum of its current value and {\ttfamily max\+\_\+v}. The update is performed using a relaxed memory ordering for efficiency in non-\/synchronizing contexts.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em T} & The type of the atomic variable. Must be trivially copyable and comparable. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em v} & The atomic variable to update. \\
\hline
{\em max\+\_\+v} & The value to compare with the current value of {\ttfamily v}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
If multiple threads call this function concurrently, the value of {\ttfamily v} will be the maximum value seen across all threads. 
\end{DoxyAttention}
\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a512ffa0d24a237b098f5de656b8bdcb0}\index{tf@{tf}!atomic\_min@{atomic\_min}}

updates an atomic variable with the minimum value 

This function atomically updates the provided atomic variable {\ttfamily v} to hold the minimum of its current value and {\ttfamily min\+\_\+v}. The update is performed using a relaxed memory ordering for efficiency in non-\/synchronizing contexts.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyAttention}

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a15c9131faea47635a65e6caf21b6f868}\index{tf@{tf}!coprime@{coprime}}
\index{coprime@{coprime}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{coprime()}{coprime()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a15c9131faea47635a65e6caf21b6f868} 
size\+\_\+t tf\+::coprime (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{N}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [constexpr]}}



computes a coprime of a given number 

This function finds the largest number less than N that is coprime (i.\+e., has a greatest common divisor of 1) with {\ttfamily N}. If {\ttfamily N} is less than 3, it returns 1 as a default coprime.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em N} & input number for which a coprime is to be found. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
the largest number \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} {\ttfamily N} that is coprime to N 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a0b8e46604b2d40f0a7f2cc4796003d49}\index{tf@{tf}!ctz@{ctz}}
\index{ctz@{ctz}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ctz()}{ctz()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a0b8e46604b2d40f0a7f2cc4796003d49} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, typename = std\+::enable\+\_\+if\+\_\+t$<$std\+::is\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+v$<$\+T$>$$>$$>$ \\
auto tf\+::ctz (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}}]{x}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



counts the number of trailing zeros in an integer. 

This function provides a portable implementation for counting the number of trailing zeros across different platforms and integer sizes (32-\/bit and 64-\/bit).


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em T} & integer type (32-\/bit or 64-\/bit). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em x} & non-\/zero integer to count trailing zeros from \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
the number of trailing zeros in {\ttfamily x} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
The behavior is undefined when {\ttfamily x} is 0. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a5f9dabd7c5d0fa5166cf76d9fa5a038e} 
template$<$typename P, typename I, typename U$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::cuda\+\_\+find\+\_\+if (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{p}{, }\item[{I}]{first}{, }\item[{I}]{last}{, }\item[{unsigned \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{idx}{, }\item[{U}]{op}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



finds the index of the first element that satisfies the given criteria 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em P} & execution policy type \\
\hline
{\em I} & input iterator type \\
\hline
{\em U} & unary operator type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em p} & execution policy \\
\hline
{\em first} & iterator to the beginning of the range \\
\hline
{\em last} & iterator to the end of the range \\
\hline
{\em idx} & pointer to the index of the found element \\
\hline
{\em op} & unary operator which returns {\ttfamily true} for the required element\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The function launches kernels asynchronously to find the index {\ttfamily idx} of the first element in the range {\ttfamily \mbox{[}first, last)} such that {\ttfamily op(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}(first+idx))} is true. This is equivalent to the parallel execution of the following loop\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ idx\ =\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(;\ first\ !=\ last;\ ++first,\ ++idx)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{main-override_8cpp_a117104b82864d3b23ec174af6d392709}{p}}(*first))\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ idx;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ idx;}

\end{DoxyCode}

\item cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Type\+Memcpy = 0x01
\item cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Type\+Memset = 0x02
\item cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Type\+Host = 0x03
\item cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Type\+Graph = 0x04
\item cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Type\+Empty = 0x05
\item cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Type\+Wait\+Event = 0x06
\item cuda\+Graph\+Node\+Type\+Event\+Record = 0x07

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a3fc577fd0a8f127770bcf68bc56c073e}\index{tf@{tf}!cuda\_max\_element@{cuda\_max\_element}}
\index{cuda\_max\_element@{cuda\_max\_element}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuda\_max\_element()}{cuda\_max\_element()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a3fc577fd0a8f127770bcf68bc56c073e} 
template$<$typename P, typename I, typename O$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::cuda\+\_\+max\+\_\+element (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{p}{, }\item[{I}]{first}{, }\item[{I}]{last}{, }\item[{unsigned \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{idx}{, }\item[{O}]{op}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{buf}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



finds the index of the maximum element in a range 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em P} & execution policy type \\
\hline
{\em I} & input iterator type \\
\hline
{\em O} & comparator type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em p} & execution policy object \\
\hline
{\em first} & iterator to the beginning of the range \\
\hline
{\em last} & iterator to the end of the range \\
\hline
{\em idx} & solution index of the maximum element \\
\hline
{\em op} & comparison function object \\
\hline
{\em buf} & pointer to the buffer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The function launches kernels asynchronously to find the largest element in the range {\ttfamily \mbox{[}first, last)} using the given comparator {\ttfamily op}. You need to provide a buffer that holds at least tf\+::cuda\+\_\+max\+\_\+element\+\_\+bufsz bytes for internal use. The function is equivalent to a parallel execution of the following loop\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(first\ ==\ last)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\ largest\ =\ first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ (++first;\ first\ !=\ last;\ ++first)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (op(*largest,\ *first))\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ largest\ =\ first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ std::distance(first,\ largest);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 函数调用图\+:

The memory areas may not overlap. \Hypertarget{namespacetf_a6615554d2954e895755411ee444d9760}\index{tf@{tf}!cuda\_memset\_async@{cuda\_memset\_async}}

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_aa84d4c68d2cbe9f6efc4a1eb1a115458}\index{tf@{tf}!cuda\_merge\_by\_key@{cuda\_merge\_by\_key}}
\index{cuda\_merge\_by\_key@{cuda\_merge\_by\_key}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuda\_merge\_by\_key()}{cuda\_merge\_by\_key()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_aa84d4c68d2cbe9f6efc4a1eb1a115458} 
template$<$typename P, typename a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it, typename a\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it, typename b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it, typename b\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it, typename c\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it, typename c\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::cuda\+\_\+merge\+\_\+by\+\_\+key (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{p}{, }\item[{a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it}]{a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it}]{a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last}{, }\item[{a\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it}]{a\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it}]{b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it}]{b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last}{, }\item[{b\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it}]{b\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{c\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it}]{c\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{c\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it}]{c\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}}]{comp}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{buf}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



performs asynchronous key-\/value merge over a range of keys and values 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em P} & execution policy type \\
\hline
{\em a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it} & first key iterator type \\
\hline
{\em a\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it} & first value iterator type \\
\hline
{\em b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it} & second key iterator type \\
\hline
{\em b\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it} & second value iterator type \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+keys\+\_\+it} & output key iterator type \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+vals\+\_\+it} & output value iterator type \\
\hline
{\em C} & comparator type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em p} & execution policy \\
\hline
{\em a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the first key range \\
\hline
{\em a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last} & iterator to the end of the first key range \\
\hline
{\em a\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the first value range \\
\hline
{\em b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the second key range \\
\hline
{\em b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last} & iterator to the end of the second key range \\
\hline
{\em b\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the second value range \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the output key range \\
\hline
{\em c\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the output value range \\
\hline
{\em comp} & comparator \\
\hline
{\em buf} & pointer to the temporary buffer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Performs a key-\/value merge that copies elements from {\ttfamily \mbox{[}a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first, a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last)} and {\ttfamily \mbox{[}b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first, b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last)} into a single range, {\ttfamily \mbox{[}c\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first, c\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last + (a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last -\/ a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first) + (b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last -\/ b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first))} such that the resulting range is in ascending key order.

At the same time, the merge copies elements from the two associated ranges {\ttfamily \mbox{[}a\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first + (a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last -\/ a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first))} and {\ttfamily \mbox{[}b\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first + (b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last -\/ b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first))} into a single range, {\ttfamily \mbox{[}c\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first, c\+\_\+vals\+\_\+first + (a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last -\/ a\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first) + (b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+last -\/ b\+\_\+keys\+\_\+first))} such that the resulting range is in ascending order implied by each input element\textquotesingle{}s associated key.

For example, assume\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily a\+\_\+keys} = \{1, 8\};
\item {\ttfamily a\+\_\+vals} = \{2, 1\};
\item {\ttfamily b\+\_\+keys} = \{3, 7\};
\item {\ttfamily b\+\_\+vals} = \{3, 4\};
\end{DoxyItemize}

After the merge, we have\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily c\+\_\+keys} = \{1, 3, 7, 8\}
\item {\ttfamily c\+\_\+vals} = \{2, 3, 4, 1\} 
\end{DoxyItemize}函数调用图\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuda\_min\_element()}{cuda\_min\_element()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a572c13198191c46765264f8afabe2e9f} 
template$<$typename P, typename I, typename O$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::cuda\+\_\+min\+\_\+element (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{p}{, }\item[{I}]{first}{, }\item[{I}]{last}{, }\item[{unsigned \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{idx}{, }\item[{O}]{op}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{buf}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



finds the index of the minimum element in a range 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em P} & execution policy type \\
\hline
{\em I} & input iterator type \\
\hline
{\em O} & comparator type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em p} & execution policy object \\
\hline
{\em first} & iterator to the beginning of the range \\
\hline
{\em last} & iterator to the end of the range \\
\hline
{\em idx} & solution index of the minimum element \\
\hline
{\em op} & comparison function object \\
\hline
{\em buf} & pointer to the buffer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The function launches kernels asynchronously to find the smallest element in the range {\ttfamily \mbox{[}first, last)} using the given comparator {\ttfamily op}. You need to provide a buffer that holds at least tf\+::cuda\+\_\+min\+\_\+element\+\_\+bufsz bytes for internal use. The function is equivalent to a parallel execution of the following loop\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(first\ ==\ last)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{auto}\ smallest\ =\ first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{for}\ (++first;\ first\ !=\ last;\ ++first)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (op(*first,\ *smallest))\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ smallest\ =\ first;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ std::distance(first,\ smallest);}

\end{DoxyCode}
 函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a3461b9179221dd7230ce2a0e45156c7f}\index{tf@{tf}!cuda\_sort\_by\_key@{cuda\_sort\_by\_key}}
\index{cuda\_sort\_by\_key@{cuda\_sort\_by\_key}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuda\_sort\_by\_key()}{cuda\_sort\_by\_key()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a3461b9179221dd7230ce2a0e45156c7f} 
template$<$typename P, typename K\+\_\+it, typename V\+\_\+it, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::cuda\+\_\+sort\+\_\+by\+\_\+key (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{p}{, }\item[{K\+\_\+it}]{k\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{K\+\_\+it}]{k\+\_\+last}{, }\item[{V\+\_\+it}]{v\+\_\+first}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}}]{comp}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{buf}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



performs asynchronous key-\/value sort on a range of items 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em P} & execution policy type \\
\hline
{\em K\+\_\+it} & key iterator type \\
\hline
{\em V\+\_\+it} & value iterator type \\
\hline
{\em C} & comparator type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em p} & execution policy \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the key range \\
\hline
{\em k\+\_\+last} & iterator to the end of the key range \\
\hline
{\em v\+\_\+first} & iterator to the beginning of the value range \\
\hline
{\em comp} & binary comparator \\
\hline
{\em buf} & pointer to the temporary buffer\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Sorts key-\/value elements in {\ttfamily \mbox{[}k\+\_\+first, k\+\_\+last)} and {\ttfamily \mbox{[}v\+\_\+first, v\+\_\+first + (k\+\_\+last -\/ k\+\_\+first))} into ascending key order using the given comparator {\ttfamily comp}. If {\ttfamily i} and {\ttfamily j} are any two valid iterators in {\ttfamily \mbox{[}k\+\_\+first, k\+\_\+last)} such that {\ttfamily i} precedes {\ttfamily j}, and {\ttfamily p} and {\ttfamily q} are iterators in {\ttfamily \mbox{[}v\+\_\+first, v\+\_\+first + (k\+\_\+last -\/ k\+\_\+first))} corresponding to {\ttfamily i} and {\ttfamily j} respectively, then {\ttfamily comp(\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}j, \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}i)} evaluates to {\ttfamily false}.

For example, assume\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily keys} are {\ttfamily \{1, 4, 2, 8, 5, 7\}}
\item {\ttfamily values} are {\ttfamily \{\textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}c\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}d\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{}\}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

After sort\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily keys} are {\ttfamily \{1, 2, 4, 5, 7, 8\}}
\item {\ttfamily values} are {\ttfamily \{\textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}c\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}e\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}f\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}d\textquotesingle{}\}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}函数调用图\+:
% FIG 34

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a3ed764530620a419e3400e1f9ab6c956}

\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::cuda\+\_\+transform (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{p}{, }\item[{I}]{first}{, }\item[{I}]{last}{, }\item[{O}]{output}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}}]{op}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



performs asynchronous parallel transforms over a range of items 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}

This method is equivalent to the parallel execution of the following loop on a GPU\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{while}\ (first\ !=\ last)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ *\mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2scan_2scan_8hpp_a8390452002ecc7a0dadc5ae0dccc9b6c}{output}}++\ =\ op(*first++);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_af00f6babb0818202960cbbf0a83bd8e7}\index{tf@{tf}!distance@{distance}}
\index{distance@{distance}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{distance()}{distance()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_af00f6babb0818202960cbbf0a83bd8e7} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{sandbox_2strassen_2omp_8cpp_a4bfa035cad7c3258704669810cd5de5d}{E}}, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_aa0c5e6692c4ba3a25e31cb65dc5ee3ef}{S}}$>$ \\
std\+::enable\+\_\+if\+\_\+t$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+integral\+\_\+v$<$ std\+::decay\+\_\+t$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}} $>$ $>$ \&\&std\+::is\+\_\+integral\+\_\+v$<$ std\+::decay\+\_\+t$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sandbox_2strassen_2omp_8cpp_a4bfa035cad7c3258704669810cd5de5d}{E}} $>$ $>$ \&\&std\+::is\+\_\+integral\+\_\+v$<$ std\+::decay\+\_\+t$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_aa0c5e6692c4ba3a25e31cb65dc5ee3ef}{S}} $>$ $>$, size\+\_\+t $>$ tf\+::distance (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}}}]{beg}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sandbox_2strassen_2omp_8cpp_a4bfa035cad7c3258704669810cd5de5d}{E}}}]{end}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_aa0c5e6692c4ba3a25e31cb65dc5ee3ef}{S}}}]{step}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [constexpr]}}



calculates the number of iterations in the given index range 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_a37a83060ac796961b44991c836f083f7}{B}} & type of the beginning index \\
\hline
{\em E} & type of the ending index \\
\hline
{\em S} & type of the step size\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em beg} & starting index of the range \\
\hline
{\em end} & ending index of the range \\
\hline
{\em step} & step size to traverse the range\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
returns the number of required iterations to traverse the range
\end{DoxyReturn}
The distance of a range represents the number of required iterations to traverse the range from the beginning index to the ending index (exclusive) with the given step size.

Example 1\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Range:\ 0\ to\ 10\ with\ step\ size\ 2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ dist\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_af00f6babb0818202960cbbf0a83bd8e7}{distance}}(0,\ 10,\ 2);\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Returns\ 5,\ the\ sequence\ is\ [0,\ 2,\ 4,\ 6,\ 8]}}

\end{DoxyCode}


Example 2\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Range:\ 10\ to\ 0\ with\ step\ size\ -\/2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ dist\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_af00f6babb0818202960cbbf0a83bd8e7}{distance}}(10,\ 0,\ -\/2);\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Returns\ 5,\ the\ sequence\ is\ [10,\ 8,\ 6,\ 4,\ 2]}}

\end{DoxyCode}


Example 3\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ Range:\ 5\ to\ 20\ with\ step\ size\ 5}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ dist\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_af00f6babb0818202960cbbf0a83bd8e7}{distance}}(5,\ 20,\ 5);\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Returns\ 3,\ the\ sequence\ is\ [5,\ 10,\ 15]}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
It is user\textquotesingle{}s responsibility to ensure the given index range is valid. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

computes the floor of the base-\/2 logarithm of a number using count-\/leading-\/zeros (CTL).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_env()}{get\_env()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_abbef08f01c467fd4f746c3247af892bc} 
std\+::string tf\+::get\+\_\+env (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::string \&}]{str}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



retrieves the value of an environment variable 

This function fetches the value of an environment variable by name. If the variable is not found, it returns an empty string.


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em str} & The name of the environment variable to retrieve. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The value of the environment variable as a string, or an empty string if not found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
The implementation differs between Windows and POSIX platforms\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item On Windows, it uses {\ttfamily \+\_\+dupenv\+\_\+s} to fetch the value.
\item On POSIX, it uses {\ttfamily std\+::getenv}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyAttention}

checks if the given index range is invalid 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} range is considered invalid under the following conditions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The step is zero and the begin and end values are not equal.
\item \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} positive range (begin \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} end) with a non-\/positive step.
\item \doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} negative range (begin \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} end) with a non-\/negative step. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a8d48a5014f34a9f97aae5269c2367e38}\index{tf@{tf}!is\_pow2@{is\_pow2}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a5233c743d9f9f17fd27373aef11fa752} 
template$<$size\+\_\+t N$>$ \\
std\+::array$<$ size\+\_\+t, \mbox{\hyperlink{main-override-static_8c_a0240ac851181b84ac374872dc5434ee4}{N}} $>$ tf\+::make\+\_\+coprime\+\_\+lut (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [constexpr]}}



generates a compile-\/time array of coprimes for numbers from 0 to N-\/1 

This function constructs a constexpr array where each element at index {\ttfamily i} contains a coprime of {\ttfamily i} (the largest number less than {\ttfamily i} that is coprime to it).


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em N} & the size of the array to generate (should be greater than 0). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
a constexpr array of size {\ttfamily N} where each index holds a coprime of its value. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a8975fa5762088789adb0b60f38208309}\index{tf@{tf}!make\_data\_pipe@{make\_data\_pipe}}
\index{make\_data\_pipe@{make\_data\_pipe}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_data\_pipe()}{make\_data\_pipe()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a8975fa5762088789adb0b60f38208309} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_input}{Input}}, typename Output, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}$>$ \\
auto tf\+::make\+\_\+data\+\_\+pipe (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_abb7a11e41fd457f69e7ff45d4c769564}{Pipe\+Type}}}]{d}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}} \&\&}]{callable}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



function to construct a data pipe (\doxylink{classtf_1_1_data_pipe}{tf\+::\+Data\+Pipe}) 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em \doxylink{struct_input}{Input}} & input data type \\
\hline
{\em Output} & output data type \\
\hline
{\em C} & callable type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\doxylink{namespacetf_a8975fa5762088789adb0b60f38208309}{tf\+::make\+\_\+data\+\_\+pipe} is a helper function to create a data pipe (\doxylink{classtf_1_1_data_pipe}{tf\+::\+Data\+Pipe}) in a data-\/parallel pipeline (\doxylink{classtf_1_1_data_pipeline}{tf\+::\+Data\+Pipeline}). The first argument specifies the direction of the data pipe, either \doxylink{namespacetf_abb7a11e41fd457f69e7ff45d4c769564a7b804a28d6154ab8007287532037f1d0}{tf\+::\+Pipe\+Type\+::\+SERIAL} or \doxylink{namespacetf_abb7a11e41fd457f69e7ff45d4c769564adf13a99b035d6f0bce4f44ab18eec8eb}{tf\+::\+Pipe\+Type\+::\+PARALLEL}, and the second argument is a callable to invoke by the pipeline scheduler. \doxylink{struct_input}{Input} and output data types are specified via template parameters, which will always be decayed by the library to its original form for storage purpose. The callable must take the input data type in its first argument and returns a value of the output data type.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_a8975fa5762088789adb0b60f38208309}{tf::make\_data\_pipe<int,\ std::string>}}(}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_abb7a11e41fd457f69e7ff45d4c769564a7b804a28d6154ab8007287532037f1d0}{tf::PipeType::SERIAL}},\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ [](\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2scan_2scan_8hpp_ab7e6955a695fad0be513586926040b1a}{input}})\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ std::to\_string(\mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2scan_2scan_8hpp_ab7e6955a695fad0be513586926040b1a}{input}}\ +\ 100);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{);}

\end{DoxyCode}


The callable can additionally take a reference of \doxylink{classtf_1_1_pipeflow}{tf\+::\+Pipeflow}, which allows you to query the runtime information of a stage task, such as its line number and token number.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_module\_task()}{make\_module\_task()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a767288f0f103fec9a849237865198627} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}$>$ \\
auto tf\+::make\+\_\+module\+\_\+task (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}} \&\&}]{target}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



creates a module task using the given target 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em T} & \doxylink{ir__common_8h_a1ac75f8fee198af783521627f1fecfbc}{Type} of the target object, which must define the method {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf\+::\+Graph}\& graph()}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em target} & The target object used to create the module task. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
module task that can be used by Taskflow or asynchronous tasking.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This example demonstrates how to create and launch multiple taskflows in parallel using asynchronous tasking\+:

\end{DoxyCode}


The module task maker, \doxylink{namespacetf_a767288f0f103fec9a849237865198627}{tf\+::make\+\_\+module\+\_\+task}, is basically the same as \doxylink{classtf_1_1_flow_builder_ac6f22228d4c2ea2e643c4b0d42c0e92a}{tf\+::\+Taskflow\+::composed\+\_\+of} but provides a more generic interface that can be used beyond Taskflow. For instance, the following two approaches achieve the same functionality.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ approach\ 1:\ composition\ using\ composed\_of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_task}{tf::Task}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_i_o_format_8cpp_ade6f22163da3c189aade978b48a8bb74}{m1}}\ =\ taskflow1.composed\_of(taskflow2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ approach\ 2:\ composition\ using\ make\_module\_task}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_task}{tf::Task}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{_i_o_format_8cpp_ade6f22163da3c189aade978b48a8bb74}{m1}}\ =\ taskflow1.emplace(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_a767288f0f103fec9a849237865198627}{tf::make\_module\_task}}(taskflow2));}

\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
Users are responsible for ensuring that the given target remains valid throughout its execution. The executor does not assume ownership of the target object. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

Rand\+Itr tf\+::median\+\_\+of\+\_\+three (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Rand\+Itr}]{l}{, }\item[{Rand\+Itr}]{m}{, }\item[{Rand\+Itr}]{r}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}}]{cmp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



finds the median of three numbers pointed to by iterators using the given comparator 

This function determines the median value of the elements pointed to by three random-\/access iterators using the provided comparator.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em Rand\+Itr} & The type of the random-\/access iterator. \\
\hline
{\em C} & The type of the comparator. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em l} & Iterator to the first element. \\
\hline
{\em m} & Iterator to the second element. \\
\hline
{\em r} & Iterator to the third element. \\
\hline
{\em cmp} & The comparator used to compare the dereferenced iterator values. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The iterator pointing to the median value among the three elements. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

% FIG 65
\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a3430ee9958ddb3ed09424e30475d9e2d}\index{tf@{tf}!pause@{pause}}
\index{pause@{pause}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pause()}{pause()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a3430ee9958ddb3ed09424e30475d9e2d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::pause (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}

This function is used in spin-\/wait loops to hint the CPU that the current thread is in a busy-\/wait state. It helps reduce power consumption and improves performance on hyper-\/threaded processors by preventing the CPU from consuming unnecessary cycles while waiting. It is particularly useful in low-\/contention scenarios, where the thread is likely to quickly acquire the lock or condition it\textquotesingle{}s waiting for, avoiding an expensive context switch. On modern x86 processors, this instruction can be invoked using {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+builtin\+\_\+ia32\+\_\+pause()} in GCC/\+Clang or {\ttfamily \+\_\+mm\+\_\+pause()} in MSVC. In non-\/x86 architectures, alternative mechanisms such as yielding the CPU may be used instead. \Hypertarget{namespacetf_ae9b372cf6337d0fd563fecc59a1915cc}\index{tf@{tf}!pause@{pause}}
\index{pause@{pause}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{pause()}{pause()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_ae9b372cf6337d0fd563fecc59a1915cc} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::pause (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{count}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



pause CPU for a specified number of iterations 

函数调用图\+:

template$<$typename Rand\+Itr, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}$>$ \\
Rand\+Itr tf\+::pseudo\+\_\+median\+\_\+of\+\_\+nine (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Rand\+Itr}]{beg}{, }\item[{Rand\+Itr}]{end}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_aaee470c3acb6b181fd804d072284fbaa}{C}}}]{cmp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



finds the pseudo median of a range of items using a spread of nine numbers 

This function computes an approximate median of a range of items by sampling nine values spread across the range and finding their median. It uses a combination of the {\ttfamily median\+\_\+of\+\_\+three} function to determine the pseudo median.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em Rand\+Itr} & The type of the random-\/access iterator. \\
\hline
{\em C} & The type of the comparator. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em beg} & Iterator to the beginning of the range. \\
\hline
{\em end} & Iterator to the end of the range. \\
\hline
{\em cmp} & The comparator used to compare the dereferenced iterator values. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
The iterator pointing to the pseudo median of the range.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
The pseudo median is an approximation of the true median and may not be the exact middle value of the range. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

template$<$typename Iter, typename Compare$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::sort3 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Iter}]{a}{, }\item[{Iter}]{b}{, }\item[{Iter}]{c}{, }\item[{Compare}]{comp}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sorts three elements of dereferenced iterators using the given comparison function. 

This function sorts three elements pointed to by iterators in ascending order according to the provided comparator. The sorting is performed using a sequence of calls to the {\ttfamily sort2} function to ensure the correct order of elements.

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a3abe09ef55c4f46e64ba88bff175c4f6}\index{tf@{tf}!spin\_until@{spin\_until}}
\index{spin\_until@{spin\_until}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{spin\_until()}{spin\_until()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a3abe09ef55c4f46e64ba88bff175c4f6} 
template$<$typename P$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tf\+::spin\+\_\+until (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{P \&\&}]{predicate}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



spins until the given predicate becomes true 


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em P} & the type of the predicate function or callable. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em predicate} & the callable that returns a boolean value, which is checked in the loop.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This function repeatedly checks the provided predicate in a spin-\/wait loop and uses a backoff strategy to minimize CPU waste during the wait. Initially, it uses the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacetf_a3430ee9958ddb3ed09424e30475d9e2d}{pause()}} instruction for the first 100 iterations to hint to the CPU that the thread is waiting, thus reducing power consumption and avoiding unnecessary cycles. After 100 iterations, it switches to yielding the CPU using {\ttfamily std\+::this\+\_\+thread\+::yield()} to allow other threads to run and improve system responsiveness.

The function operates as follows\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item For the first 100 iterations, it invokes {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacetf_a3430ee9958ddb3ed09424e30475d9e2d}{pause()}} to reduce power consumption during the spin-\/wait.
\item After 100 iterations, it uses {\ttfamily std\+::this\+\_\+thread\+::yield()} to relinquish the CPU, allowing other threads to execute.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
This function is useful when you need to wait for a condition to be true, but want to optimize CPU usage during the wait by using a busy-\/wait approach. 
\end{DoxyAttention}
函数调用图\+:

\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a7d5979bf44616a9019e700556aa396ba}\index{tf@{tf}!sycl\_reduce\_buffer\_size@{sycl\_reduce\_buffer\_size}}

 \Hypertarget{namespacetf_a00b75b92482d883f06282d5181e6f6f9}\index{tf@{tf}!unique\_id@{unique\_id}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_a00b75b92482d883f06282d5181e6f6f9} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, std\+::enable\+\_\+if\+\_\+t$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+integral\+\_\+v$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}} $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} $>$ \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} = nullptr$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}} tf\+::unique\+\_\+id (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



generates a program-\/wide unique ID of the given type in a thread-\/safe manner 

This function provides a globally unique identifier of the specified integral type. It uses a static {\ttfamily std\+::atomic} counter to ensure thread safety and increments the counter in a relaxed memory ordering for efficiency.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em T} & The type of the ID to generate. Must be an integral type. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} unique ID of type {\ttfamily T}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
The uniqueness of the ID is guaranteed only within the program\textquotesingle{}s lifetime. 

The function does not throw exceptions. 
\end{DoxyAttention}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetf_aea3945d9b15c96a72540ea4fe61947e7} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} tf\+::has\+\_\+graph\+\_\+v = \mbox{\hyperlink{structtf_1_1has__graph}{has\+\_\+graph}}$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}$>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [constexpr]}}



determines if the given type has a member function {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{Graph}\& graph()} 

This trait determines if the provided type {\ttfamily T} contains a member function with the exact signature {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf\+::\+Graph}\& graph()}. It uses SFINAE and {\ttfamily std\+::void\+\_\+t} to detect the presence of the member function and its return type.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{模板参数}
{\em T} & The type to inspect. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{返回值}
{\em true} & If the type {\ttfamily T} has a member function {\ttfamily \doxylink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf\+::\+Graph}\& graph()}. \\
\hline
{\em false} & Otherwise.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
Example usage\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf::Graph}}\&\ graph()\ \{\ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ my\_graph;\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classtf_1_1_graph}{tf::Graph}}\ my\_graph;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ other\ custom\ members\ to\ alter\ my\_graph}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{test__buffer__node_8cpp_ac4cf4b2ab929bd23951a8676eeac086b}{C}}\ \{\};\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ No\ graph\ function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{static\_assert}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_aea3945d9b15c96a72540ea4fe61947e7}{has\_graph\_v<A>}},\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}A\ has\ graph()"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{static\_assert}(!\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetf_aea3945d9b15c96a72540ea4fe61947e7}{has\_graph\_v<C>}},\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}C\ does\ not\ have\ graph()"{}});}

\end{DoxyCode}

determines if a callable is a dynamic task 

\doxylink{bench__gemm_8cpp_addc86e8508f14411ec98f521c520f875}{A} dynamic task is a callable object constructible from std\+::function$<$void(\+Subflow\&)$>$. \Hypertarget{namespacetf_ad3a41adc2499a9519da3e77dc3e9849c}\index{tf@{tf}!is\_task\_params\_v@{is\_task\_params\_v}}
\index{is\_task\_params\_v@{is\_task\_params\_v}!tf@{tf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{is\_task\_params\_v}{is\_task\_params\_v}}

{\bfseries 初始值\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{=}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ std::is\_same\_v<std::decay\_t<P>,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structtf_1_1_task_params}{TaskParams}}>\ ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ std::is\_same\_v<std::decay\_t<P>,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structtf_1_1_default_task_params}{DefaultTaskParams}}>\ ||}

\end{DoxyCode}


determines if the given type is a task parameter type 

\doxylink{classtf_1_1_task}{Task} parameters can be specified in one of the following types\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{structtf_1_1_task_params}{tf\+::\+Task\+Params}\+: assign the struct of defined parameters
\item \doxylink{structtf_1_1_default_task_params}{tf\+::\+Default\+Task\+Params}\+: assign nothing
\item std\+::string\+: assign a name to the task 
\end{DoxyItemize}\Hypertarget{namespacetf_a40de533868648566e76c2495fbbfba70}\index{tf@{tf}!SYCL\_WARP\_SIZE@{SYCL\_WARP\_SIZE}}
